Key and Explanation
High Risk One or More Critical Violations (9 points each)
Low Risk No Critical Violations and a score of 90 or above
 
  • Violations marked in bold are Critical Violations
  • If a restaurant receives a failing score for an inspection, a score of less than 70, then they will receive a follow-up inspection within 10 days
  • Roll your mouse over the violation text to view the inspector's observations
  • Click a column header to resort on that column
